   77     <p class="section-sub">HVAC systems are mechanical — they wear down ove
      r time. Regular maintenance is the single most effective thing you can do t
      o extend equipment life, maintain efficiency, and avoid costly emergency ca
      lls.</p>
   78   </div>
   79   <div class="cards-grid">

   83       <p class="detail-card-text">A dirty, neglected system works harder an
      d uses more energy. Regular tune-ups keep your equipment operating at rated
       efficiency — which shows up on your utility bill every month.</p>
   84     </div>
   85     <div class="detail-card">
   86       <div class="detail-card-icon">&#128336;</div>
   87       <div class="detail-card-title">Longer System Life</div>

      5–10 years longer on average. That's thousands of dollars in delayed replac
      ement costs — just from regular tune-ups.</p>
   89     </div>
   90     <div class="detail-card">

      omponents before they cause a breakdown — especially important before peak
      heating and cooling season.</p>

   95     <div class="detail-card">

  215     <div class="faq-list">
  216       <details class="faq-item">
  217         <summary class="faq-q">When should I schedule my tune-up?<span clas
      s="faq-toggle">+</span></summary>
  218         <p class="faq-a">Fall (September–October) for heating systems, spri
      ng (April–May) for cooling. The key is getting it done before peak season —
       not during it, when technicians are busiest.</p>
  219       </details>

      that only a trained technician will notice — worn components, efficiency de
      gradation, or safety issues. Prevention is always cheaper than emergency re
      pair.</p>

  227       </details>

   63     <h1 class="page-hero-title">HVAC Maintenance Agreements<br>for <span class="red">Ocean County Homeowners</span></h1>
   64     <p class="page-hero-desc">The best time to find a problem with your heating or cooling system is before it becomes an emergency. Sheridan's maintenance agreements keep your equipment running at pe
      ak efficiency — and give you one less thing to worry about.</p>
   65     <div class="page-hero-btns">

   72 <!-- WHY MAINTENANCE MATTERS -->
   73 <section class="section-pad bg-white">
   74   <div class="text-center" style="max-width:680px;margin:0 auto 3rem;">
   75     <div class="section-tag">Why It Matters</div>
   76     <h2 class="section-title">The Cost of Skipping Maintenance</h2>
   77     <p class="section-sub">HVAC systems are mechanical — they wear down over time. Regular maintenance is the single most effective thing you can do to extend equipment life, maintain efficiency, and
      avoid costly emergency calls.</p>
   78   </div>
   79   <div class="cards-grid">
   80     <div class="detail-card">
   81       <div class="detail-card-icon">&#128200;</div>
   82       <div class="detail-card-title">Lower Energy Bills</div>
   83       <p class="detail-card-text">A dirty, neglected system works harder and uses more energy. Regular tune-ups keep your equipment operating at rated efficiency — which shows up on your utility bill
      every month.</p>
   84     </div>
   85     <div class="detail-card">
   86       <div class="detail-card-icon">&#128336;</div>
   87       <div class="detail-card-title">Longer System Life</div>
   88       <p class="detail-card-text">Properly maintained HVAC equipment lasts 5–10 years longer on average. That's thousands of dollars in delayed replacement costs — just from regular tune-ups.</p>
   89     </div>
   90     <div class="detail-card">
   91       <div class="detail-card-icon">&#9989;</div>
   92       <div class="detail-card-title">Fewer Breakdowns</div>
   93       <p class="detail-card-text">Most system failures don't happen without warning. Our technicians catch worn belts, failing capacitors, and dirty components before they cause a breakdown — especial
      ly important before peak heating and cooling season.</p>
   94     </div>
   95     <div class="detail-card">
   96       <div class="detail-card-icon">&#128274;</div>
   97       <div class="detail-card-title">Warranty Protection</div>
   98       <p class="detail-card-text">Many equipment manufacturers require documented annual maintenance to keep the warranty valid. Our maintenance agreements provide that documentation automatically.</p
      >
   99     </div>
  100     <div class="detail-card">
  101       <div class="detail-card-icon">&#128168;</div>
  102       <div class="detail-card-title">Safer Operation</div>
  103       <p class="detail-card-text">Gas furnaces and boilers require safety checks — heat exchangers, flue systems, and carbon monoxide risks. Annual tune-ups include safety inspections that protect you
      r family.</p>
  104     </div>
  105     <div class="detail-card">
  106       <div class="detail-card-icon">&#128640;</div>
  107       <div class="detail-card-title">Priority Service</div>
  108       <p class="detail-card-text">Maintenance agreement customers move to the front of the line for service calls. When your heat fails in January and we're booking fast, you'll be glad you signed up.
      </p>
  109     </div>

  166       <h2 class="section-title">A Thorough Visit Every Time</h2>
  167       <p class="section-sub">Our maintenance visits aren't a 15-minute check of a few boxes. We take our time and inspect the entire system — because that's the only way to actually protect your equip
      ment.</p>
  168       <ul class="service-list">
  169         <li>Inspect and clean heat exchanger (gas systems)</li>
  170         <li>Test and clean burners for proper ignition and combustion</li>
  171         <li>Check flue and venting for blockages or damage</li>
  172         <li>Inspect and lubricate all moving parts</li>
  173         <li>Test safety controls and limit switches</li>
  174         <li>Check refrigerant levels and look for leaks (AC)</li>
  175         <li>Clean evaporator and condenser coils</li>
  176         <li>Inspect electrical connections and components</li>
  177         <li>Test thermostat calibration and operation</li>
  178         <li>Check and clear condensate drain lines</li>

  216       <details class="faq-item">
  217         <summary class="faq-q">When should I schedule my tune-up?<span class="faq-toggle">+</span></summary>
  218         <p class="faq-a">Fall (September–October) for heating systems, spring (April–May) for cooling. The key is getting it done before peak season — not during it, when technicians are busiest.</p>
  219       </details>
  220       <details class="faq-item">
  221         <summary class="faq-q">My system seems fine — do I still need maintenance?<span class="faq-toggle">+</span></summary>
  222         <p class="faq-a">Absolutely. Most HVAC failures give warning signs that only a trained technician will notice — worn components, efficiency degradation, or safety issues. Prevention is always
      cheaper than emergency repair.</p>
  223       </details>
  224       <details class="faq-item">
  225         <summary class="faq-q">Do you service all brands?<span class="faq-toggle">+</span></summary>
  226         <p class="faq-a">Yes. We maintain and service all major brands including Trane, Carrier, Lennox, Rheem, York, Goodman, Weil-McLain, Burnham, and more. We service what you have.</p>
  227       </details>
  228       <details class="faq-item">
  229         <summary class="faq-q">What's the difference between a tune-up and a service call?<span class="faq-toggle">+</span></summary>
  230         <p class="faq-a">A tune-up is proactive — we inspect, clean, and adjust your system to keep it running well. A service call is reactive — you call us because something broke. Tune-ups are much
       cheaper than service calls.</p>
  231       </details>
  232       <details class="faq-item">
  233         <summary class="faq-q">Can I cancel the agreement?<span class="faq-toggle">+</span></summary>
  234         <p class="faq-a">Yes — we want customers who want to be here. Ask about our cancellation policy when you sign up. We keep it simple and fair.</p>

  101       <h2 class="section-title">Built in Southern Ocean County, for Southern Ocean County</h2>
  102       <p class="section-sub" style="margin-bottom:1.2rem;">Chris Sheridan started this company in 1995 with a truck, a set of tools, and a commitment to treating every customer like a neighbor — becau
      se in Little Egg Harbor, they often are.</p>
  103       <p style="font-size:0.9rem;color:var(--gray);line-height:1.75;margin-bottom:1.2rem;">What began as a one-man operation has grown into a trusted name across Ocean County and the Jersey Shore. We'
      ve installed and serviced HVAC systems in thousands of homes — from year-round residences to LBI vacation properties, from post-Sandy rebuilds to new construction.</p>
  104       <p style="font-size:0.9rem;color:var(--gray);line-height:1.75;margin-bottom:1.5rem;">We don't advertise much. We don't need to. Our work speaks for itself, and our customers speak for us — in 5-
      star Google reviews, Nextdoor recommendations, and word of mouth that has carried us for three decades.</p>

  297 /* Simple Formspree success handler */
  298 var form = document.getElementById('contactForm');
  299 if (form) {
  300   form.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
  301     /* If Formspree isn't set up yet, show the message anyway for demo purp
      oses */
  302     if (form.action.includes('YOUR_FORM_ID')) {
  303       e.preventDefault();
  304       document.getElementById('successMsg').style.display = 'block';
  305       form.reset();
  306     }
  307   });
  308 }

  297 /* Simple Formspree success handler */
  298 var form = document.getElementById('contactForm');
  299 if (form) {
  300   form.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
  301     /* If Formspree isn't set up yet, show the message anyway for demo purposes */
  302     if (form.action.includes('YOUR_FORM_ID')) {
  303       e.preventDefault();
